${{\partial{v^2}}\over{\partial v_x}} = {{{2}} {{{v_x}}}}$
${{\partial{v^2}}\over{\partial v_y}} = {{{2}} {{{v_y}}}}$
${{\partial{v^2}}\over{\partial v_z}} = {{{2}} {{{v_z}}}}$
${W} = {\frac{1}{\sqrt{{1} - {{v^2}}}}}$
${{1} - {{v^2}}} = {\frac{1}{{W}^{2}}}$
${{\partial W}\over{\partial v_x}} = {{{{v_x}}} \cdot {{{W}^{3}}}}$
${{\partial W}\over{\partial v_y}} = {{{{v_y}}} \cdot {{{W}^{3}}}}$
${{\partial W}\over{\partial v_z}} = {{{{v_z}}} \cdot {{{W}^{3}}}}$
${P} = {{{{{({{\gamma} - {1}})}} {{\rho}}}} {{{e_{int}}}}}$
${{\partial P}\over{\partial\rho}} = {{{{e_{int}}}} \cdot {{({{-{1}} + {\gamma}})}}}$
${{\partial P}\over{\partial e_{int}}} = {{{\rho}} \cdot {{({{-{1}} + {\gamma}})}}}$

${h} = {{{1} + {{e_{int}}}} + {{\frac{1}{\rho}}{({P})}}}$
${h} = {{1} + {{{\gamma}} \cdot {{{e_{int}}}}}}$
${{\partial h}\over{\partial e_{int}}} = {\gamma}$
${D} = {{{\rho}} \cdot {{W}}}$
${D} = {{{\rho}} \cdot {{\frac{1}{\sqrt{{1} - {{v^2}}}}}}}$
${ \left[ \begin{matrix} {S_x} \\ {S_y} \\ {S_z} \end{matrix} \right] } = { \left[ \begin{matrix} {{\rho}} \cdot {{h}} {{{W}^{2}}} {{{v_x}}} \\ {{\rho}} \cdot {{h}} {{{W}^{2}}} {{{v_y}}} \\ {{\rho}} \cdot {{h}} {{{W}^{2}}} {{{v_z}}} \end{matrix} \right] }$
${\tau} = {{E} - {D}}$
${\tau} = {{{{{{{\rho}} \cdot {{h}}}} {{{W}^{2}}}} - {P}} - {D}}$
${U} = { \left[ \begin{matrix} D \\ {S_x} \\ {S_y} \\ {S_z} \\ \tau \end{matrix} \right] }$
${{F_x}} = { \left[ \begin{matrix} {{D}} {{{v_x}}} \\ {{{{S_x}}} \cdot {{{v_x}}}} - {P} \\ {{{S_y}}} \cdot {{{v_x}}} \\ {{{S_z}}} \cdot {{{v_x}}} \\ {{S_x}} - {{{D}} {{{v_x}}}} \end{matrix} \right] }$
${{\partial D}\over{\partial\rho}} = {W}$
${ \left[ \begin{matrix} {\partial D}\over{\partial v_x} \\ {\partial D}\over{\partial v_y} \\ {\partial D}\over{\partial v_z} \end{matrix} \right] } = { \left[ \begin{matrix} {{\rho}} \cdot {{{{{v_x}}} \cdot {{{W}^{3}}}}} \\ {{\rho}} \cdot {{{{{v_y}}} \cdot {{{W}^{3}}}}} \\ {{\rho}} \cdot {{{{{v_z}}} \cdot {{{W}^{3}}}}} \end{matrix} \right] }$
${{\partial D}\over{\partial e_{int}}} = {0}$
${ \left[ \begin{matrix} {\partial{S_x}}\over{\partial\rho} \\ {\partial{S_y}}\over{\partial\rho} \\ {\partial{S_z}}\over{\partial\rho} \end{matrix} \right] } = { \left[ \begin{matrix} {{h}} {{{W}^{2}}} {{{v_x}}} \\ {{h}} {{{W}^{2}}} {{{v_y}}} \\ {{h}} {{{W}^{2}}} {{{v_z}}} \end{matrix} \right] }$
${ \left[ \begin{matrix} {\partial{S_x}}\over{\partial v_x} & {\partial{S_x}}\over{\partial v_y} & {\partial{S_x}}\over{\partial v_z} \\ {\partial{S_y}}\over{\partial v_x} & {\partial{S_y}}\over{\partial v_y} & {\partial{S_y}}\over{\partial v_z} \\ {\partial{S_z}}\over{\partial v_x} & {\partial{S_z}}\over{\partial v_y} & {\partial{S_z}}\over{\partial v_z} \end{matrix} \right] } = { \left[ \begin{matrix} {{\rho}} \cdot {{h}} {{{W}^{2}}} {{({{1} + {{{2}} {{{W}^{2}}} {{{{v_x}}^{2}}}}})}} & {{2}} {{\rho}} \cdot {{h}} {{{W}^{4}}} {{{v_x}}} \cdot {{{v_y}}} & {{2}} {{\rho}} \cdot {{h}} {{{W}^{4}}} {{{v_x}}} \cdot {{{v_z}}} \\ {{2}} {{\rho}} \cdot {{h}} {{{W}^{4}}} {{{v_y}}} \cdot {{{v_x}}} & {{\rho}} \cdot {{h}} {{{W}^{2}}} {{({{1} + {{{2}} {{{W}^{2}}} {{{{v_y}}^{2}}}}})}} & {{2}} {{\rho}} \cdot {{h}} {{{W}^{4}}} {{{v_y}}} \cdot {{{v_z}}} \\ {{2}} {{\rho}} \cdot {{h}} {{{W}^{4}}} {{{v_z}}} \cdot {{{v_x}}} & {{2}} {{\rho}} \cdot {{h}} {{{W}^{4}}} {{{v_z}}} \cdot {{{v_y}}} & {{\rho}} \cdot {{h}} {{{W}^{2}}} {{({{1} + {{{2}} {{{W}^{2}}} {{{{v_z}}^{2}}}}})}} \end{matrix} \right] }$
${ \left[ \begin{matrix} {\partial{S_x}}\over{\partial e_{int}} \\ {\partial{S_y}}\over{\partial e_{int}} \\ {\partial{S_z}}\over{\partial e_{int}} \end{matrix} \right] } = { \left[ \begin{matrix} {{\rho}} \cdot {{{W}^{2}}} {{{v_x}}} \cdot {{\gamma}} \\ {{\rho}} \cdot {{{W}^{2}}} {{{v_y}}} \cdot {{\gamma}} \\ {{\rho}} \cdot {{{W}^{2}}} {{{v_z}}} \cdot {{\gamma}} \end{matrix} \right] }$
${{\partial\tau}\over{\partial\rho}} = {-{({{{\partial D}\over{\partial\rho}} + {{{\partial P}\over{\partial\rho}} - {{{h}} {{{W}^{2}}}}}})}}$
${{\partial\tau}\over{\partial\rho}} = {-{({{{W} - {{e_{int}}}} + {{{{{e_{int}}}} \cdot {{\gamma}}} - {{{h}} {{{W}^{2}}}}}})}}$
${ \left[ \begin{matrix} {\partial\tau}\over{\partial v_x} \\ {\partial\tau}\over{\partial v_y} \\ {\partial\tau}\over{\partial v_z} \end{matrix} \right] } = { \left[ \begin{matrix} -{{{\rho}} \cdot {{{W}^{3}}} {{{v_x}}} \cdot {{({{1} - {{{2}} {{W}} {{h}}}})}}} \\ -{{{\rho}} \cdot {{{W}^{3}}} {{{v_y}}} \cdot {{({{1} - {{{2}} {{W}} {{h}}}})}}} \\ -{{{\rho}} \cdot {{{W}^{3}}} {{{v_z}}} \cdot {{({{1} - {{{2}} {{W}} {{h}}}})}}} \end{matrix} \right] }$
${{\partial\tau}\over{\partial e_{int}}} = {-{({{{\partial D}\over{\partial e_{int}}} + {{{\partial P}\over{\partial e_{int}}} - {{{\rho}} \cdot {{{\partial h}\over{\partial e_{int}}}} {{{W}^{2}}}}}})}}$
${{\partial\tau}\over{\partial e_{int}}} = {{{\rho}} \cdot {{({{1} + {{{{{W}^{2}}} {{\gamma}}} - {\gamma}}})}}}$
